<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column8008_6b38ec-ab"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading8008_10ac8d-9f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading8008_10ac8d-9f"><a href="https://www.yourgirlknows.com/about/" class="1" data-lasso-id="166580">Meet The Author</a></h2>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading8008_7a5dfa-18 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading8008_7a5dfa-18"><strong>I am Harman, your personal fashion stylist and beauty expert!</strong></h3>



<p>Hey, beauties! Welcome to the coziest, quirkiest corner of the internet. I’ve been building this space with love (and a <em>lot</em> of late-night hustle) for the past six years.</p>



<p>I’m obsessed with fashion, picky about skincare and haircare, and always down to share the real, no-filter experiences behind <strong>Your Girl Knows</strong>. Think trends, tips, ideas, honest reviews, and all the fashion-beauty tea you actually want to hear.</p>



<p>Need outfit inspo? A beauty breakdown? Styling secrets? Or just a digital bestie to help you out? I got you.</p>



<p>So grab your fave coffee (or smoothie), settle in, and let’s scroll, sip, and get fabulous together.</p>



<p>P.S. Want VIP access to my heart? Bring me something cheesy… and a cute cocktail doesn’t hurt either. 😉</p>
